<file path="infrastructure/persistence/services/EventPublishWorker.ts">
// src/application/use-cases/ports/EventPublisherWorker.ts
import { OutboxRepository } from &quot;../../../application/use-cases/ports/OutBoxRepository.js&quot;;

export class EventPublisherWorker {
  constructor(private readonly outboxRepo: OutboxRepository) {}

  async publishPending() {
    const events = await this.outboxRepo.findPending();
    for (const event of events) {
      try {
        console.log(&quot;Publicando evento:&quot;, event.eventName, event.payload);
        await this.outboxRepo.markAsPublished(event.id);
      } catch (err) {
        console.error(&quot;Error publicando evento&quot;, event.id, err);
      }
    }
  }
}
    
</file>

<file path="infrastructure/persistence/services/SubscriptionServiceImpl.ts">
import { injectable } from &quot;inversify&quot;;
import { SubscriptionService } from &quot;../../../application/use-cases/ports/SubscriptionService.js&quot;;
import { getPrismaClient } from &quot;../../persistence/prisma/PrismaClient.js&quot;;

@injectable()
export class SubscriptionServiceImpl implements SubscriptionService {
  private prisma = getPrismaClient();

  async canCreateProcess(organizationId: string): Promise&lt;boolean&gt; {
    try {
      const subscription = await this.prisma.subscription.findFirst({
        where: {
          organizationId,
          status: &quot;ACTIVE&quot;,
        },
        include: {
          plan: true,
        },
      });

      // Desarrollo:
      // si la organización aún no tiene suscripción,
      // permitimos crear procesos.

      if (!subscription) {
        console.warn(
          `[DEV] Organization ${organizationId} has no subscription. Allowing process creation.`
        );

        return true;
      }

      const activeProcesses = await this.prisma.process.count({
        where: {
          organizationId,
          status: &quot;ACTIVE&quot;,
        },
      });

      return activeProcesses &lt; subscription.plan.maxActiveProcesses;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(
        &quot;Subscription validation failed:&quot;,
        error
      );

      return false;
    }
  }
}
</file>

<file path="interfaces/http/authMiddleware.ts">
import { Request, Response, NextFunction } from &apos;express&apos;;
import jwt from &apos;jsonwebtoken&apos;;

export const authMiddleware = (req: Request, res: Response, next: NextFunction) =&gt; {
  const token = req.headers.authorization?.split(&apos; &apos;)[1];
  if (!token) return res.status(401).json({ error: &apos;No token&apos; });
  try {
    jwt.verify(token, process.env.JWT_SECRET!);
    next();
  } catch {
    res.status(401).json({ error: &apos;Invalid token&apos; });
  }
};
</file>

<file path="interfaces/http/ProcessController.ts">
import { Request, Response } from &apos;express&apos;;
import crypto from &apos;crypto&apos;;
import { z } from &apos;zod&apos;;
import { injectable, inject } from &apos;inversify&apos;;

// SOLUCIÓN A LOS ERRORES: Añadimos .js al final de las rutas locales
import { StartExecution } from &apos;../../application/use-cases/StartExecution.js&apos;;
import { CreateAndActivateProcess } from &apos;../../application/use-cases/CreateAndActivateProcess.js&apos;;
import { DomainError } from &quot;../../domain/entities/audit/shared/DomainError.js&quot;;

// Esquemas de validación
const startExecutionSchema = z.object({
  processId: z.string().uuid(),
  executionId: z.string().uuid(),
});

const createProcessSchema = z.object({
  name: z.string().min(3),
  organizationId: z.string().uuid(),
  steps: z.array(z.object({
    id: z.string().uuid(),
    name: z.string().min(1),
    order: z.number().int().min(0)
  })).min(1)
});

@injectable()
export class ProcessController {
  // Inyectamos ambos casos de uso
  constructor(
    @inject(StartExecution) private startExecUseCase: StartExecution,
    @inject(CreateAndActivateProcess) private createProcessUseCase: CreateAndActivateProcess
  ) {}

  // MÉTODO EXISTENTE: Ejecutar
  async startExecution(req: Request, res: Response): Promise&lt;void&gt; {
    try {
      const { processId, executionId } = startExecutionSchema.parse(req.body);
      await this.startExecUseCase.execute(processId, executionId);
      res.status(201).json({ executionId });;
    } catch (error) {
      this.handleError(res, error);
    }
  }

  // MÉTODO NUEVO: Crear
  async create(req: Request, res: Response): Promise&lt;void&gt; {
    try {
      const validatedData = createProcessSchema.parse(req.body);
      
      // El ID del proceso lo puede mandar el cliente o generarlo aquí
      const processId = (req.body.id as string) || crypto.randomUUID();

      await this.createProcessUseCase.execute({
        id: processId,
        ...validatedData
      });

      res.status(201).json({ id: processId, message: &quot;Process created and activated&quot; });
    } catch (error) {
      this.handleError(res, error);
    }
  }

  // Helper para no repetir código de errores
  private handleError(res: Response, error: unknown) {
    if (error instanceof z.ZodError) {
      res.status(400).json({ error: &quot;Invalid input&quot;, details: error.issues });
      return;
    }

    if (error instanceof DomainError) {
      res.status(422).json({ error: error.message });
      return;
    }

    
    console.error(&quot;🔥 Error crítico en ProcessController:&quot;, error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: &quot;Internal server error&quot; });
  }
}
</file>

<file path="interfaces/http/ProcessRoutes.ts">
import { Router } from &apos;express&apos;;
// 🚀 SOLUCIÓN A LOS ERRORES: Añadimos .js al final de las rutas locales
import { ProcessController } from &apos;./ProcessController.js&apos;;
import { container } from &apos;../../infrastructure/config/container.js&apos;;

export class ProcessRoutes {
  public router: Router;
  private controller: ProcessController;

  constructor() {
    this.router = Router();
    this.controller = container.get(ProcessController);
    this.initRoutes();
  }

  private initRoutes(): void {
    // Paso 2 del Dashboard: Procesa el POST /api/processes
    this.router.post(&apos;/&apos;, this.controller.create.bind(this.controller));
    
    // Paso 3 del Dashboard: Procesa las ejecuciones
    this.router.post(&apos;/start-execution&apos;, this.controller.startExecution.bind(this.controller));
  }
}
</file>

import { z } from &apos;zod&apos;;

export const CreateProcessSchema = z.object({
name: z.string().min(3).max(100),
  organizationId: z.string().uuid(), // En el futuro esto vendrá del token
steps: z.array(z.object({
    id: z.string().uuid(),
    name: z.string().min(1),
    order: z.number().int().min(0)
})).min(1, &quot;Un proceso debe tener al menos un paso&quot;)
});
